141→// Read and parse deduped items, assigning stable DEBT-XXXX IDs\n   142→function readAndAssignIds() {\n   143→  if (!fs.existsSync(INPUT_FILE)) {\n   144→    console.error(`❌ Input file not found: 195→\n   196→  return { items, preservedCount, newCount };\n   197→}\n   198→\n   199→// Try to find an existing stable ID for an item\n   200→function assignStableId(item, idMap, usedIds, nextId) {\n 263→\n   264→// Preserve fields from existing MASTER items during regeneration\n   265→function preserveExistingFields(item, itemMap) {\n   266→  const existing = itemMap.get(item.id);\n   267→  if
